34/**
35 * Non-regression tests for bugs fixed in Java Search engine.
36 */
37public class JavaSearchBugsTests extends AbstractJavaSearchTests implements IJavaScriptSearchConstants {
38        private final static int UI_DECLARATIONS = DECLARATIONS|IGNORE_DECLARING_TYPE|IGNORE_RETURN_TYPE;
39        
40public JavaSearchBugsTests(String name) {
41        super(name);
42        this.endChar = "";
43}
44public static Test suite() {
45        return buildModelTestSuite(JavaSearchBugsTests.class);
46}
47static {
48//        org.eclipse.wst.jsdt.internal.core.search.BasicSearchEngine.VERBOSE = true;
49//        org.eclipse.wst.jsdt.internal.codeassist.SelectionEngine.DEBUG = true;
50}
51 
52class TestCollector extends JavaSearchResultCollector {
53        public List matches = new ArrayList();
54        public void acceptSearchMatch(SearchMatch searchMatch) throws CoreException {
55                super.acceptSearchMatch(searchMatch);
56                matches.add(searchMatch);
57        }
58}
59class TypeReferencesCollector extends JavaSearchResultCollector {
60        protected IJavaScriptElement getElement(SearchMatch searchMatch) {
61                IJavaScriptElement element = super.getElement(searchMatch);
62                IJavaScriptElement localElement = null;
63                TypeReferenceMatch typeRefMatch = (TypeReferenceMatch) match;
64                localElement = typeRefMatch.getLocalElement();
65                if (localElement != null) {
66                        return localElement;
67                }
68                return element;
69        }
70        protected void writeLine() throws CoreException {
71                super.writeLine();
72                TypeReferenceMatch typeRefMatch = (TypeReferenceMatch) this.match;
73                IJavaScriptElement[] others = typeRefMatch.getOtherElements();
74                int length = others==null ? 0 : others.length;
75                if (length > 0) {
76                        line.append("+[");
77                        for (int i=0; i<length; i++) {
78                                IJavaScriptElement other = others[i];
79                                if (i>0) line.append(',');
80                                line.append(other.getElementName());
81                        }
82                        line.append(']');
83                }
84        }
85}
86 
87IJavaScriptSearchScope getJavaSearchScopeBugs() {
88        return SearchEngine.createJavaSearchScope(new IJavaScriptProject[] {getJavaProject("JavaSearchBugs")});
89}
90IJavaScriptSearchScope getJavaSearchScopeBugs(String packageName, boolean addSubpackages) throws JavaScriptModelException {
91        if (packageName == null) return getJavaSearchScopeBugs();
92        return getJavaSearchPackageScope("JavaSearchBugs", packageName, addSubpackages);
93}
94public IJavaScriptUnit getWorkingCopy(String path, String source) throws JavaScriptModelException {
95        if (this.wcOwner == null) {
96                this.wcOwner = new WorkingCopyOwner() {};
97        }
98        return getWorkingCopy(path, source, this.wcOwner, null/*don't compute problems*/);
99}
100protected void search(IJavaScriptElement element, int limitTo) throws CoreException {
101        search(element, limitTo, EXACT_RULE, getJavaSearchScopeBugs(), resultCollector);
102}
103protected void search(IJavaScriptElement element, int limitTo, int matchRule) throws CoreException {
104        search(element, limitTo, matchRule, getJavaSearchScopeBugs(), resultCollector);
105}
106protected void search(String patternString, int searchFor, int limitTo) throws CoreException {
107        search(patternString, searchFor, limitTo, EXACT_RULE, getJavaSearchScopeBugs(), resultCollector);
108}
109protected void search(String patternString, int searchFor, int limitTo, int matchRule) throws CoreException {
110        search(patternString, searchFor, limitTo, matchRule, getJavaSearchScopeBugs(), resultCollector);
111}

135/**
136 * Bug 41018: Method reference not found
137 * @see "https://bugs.eclipse.org/bugs/show_bug.cgi?id=41018"
138 */
139public void testBug41018() throws CoreException {
140        workingCopies = new IJavaScriptUnit[1];
141        workingCopies[0] = getWorkingCopy("/JavaSearchBugs/src/b41018/A.js",
142                "package b41018;\n" +
143                "public class A {\n" + 
144                "        protected void anotherMethod() {\n" + 
145                "                methodA(null);\n" + 
146                "        }\n" + 
147                "        private Object methodA(ClassB.InnerInterface arg3) {\n" + 
148                "                return null;\n" + 
149                "        }\n" + 
150                "}\n" + 
151                "class ClassB implements InterfaceB {\n" + 
152                "}\n" + 
153                "interface InterfaceB {\n" + 
154                "        interface InnerInterface {\n" + 
155                "        }\n" + 
156                "}\n"
157                );
158        IType type = workingCopies[0].getType("A");
159        IFunction method = type.getFunction("methodA", new String[] { "QClassB.InnerInterface;" });
160        search(method, REFERENCES);
161        assertSearchResults(
162                "src/b41018/A.java void b41018.A.anotherMethod() [methodA(null)] EXACT_MATCH"
163        );
164}

476/**
477 * Bug 73696: searching only works for IJavaScriptSearchConstants.TYPE, but not CLASS or INTERFACE
478 * @see "http://bugs.eclipse.org/bugs/show_bug.cgi?id=73696"
479 */
480public void testBug73696() throws CoreException {
481        workingCopies = new IJavaScriptUnit[2];
482        WorkingCopyOwner owner = new WorkingCopyOwner() {};
483        workingCopies[0] = getWorkingCopy("/JavaSearchBugs/src/b73696/C.js",
484                "package b73696;\n" + 
485                "public class C implements  I {\n" + 
486                "}",
487                owner,
488                true);
489        workingCopies[1] = getWorkingCopy("/JavaSearchBugs/src/b73696/I.js",
490                "package b73696;\n" + 
491                "public interface I {}\n",
492                owner,
493                true);
494        IJavaScriptSearchScope scope = SearchEngine.createJavaSearchScope(workingCopies);
495        
496        // Interface declaration
497        TypeDeclarationPattern pattern = new TypeDeclarationPattern(
498                null,
499                null,
500                null,
501                IIndexConstants.INTERFACE_SUFFIX,
502                SearchPattern.R_PATTERN_MATCH
503        );
504        new SearchEngine(new IJavaScriptUnit[] {workingCopies[1]}).search(
505                pattern,
506                new SearchParticipant[] {SearchEngine.getDefaultSearchParticipant()},
507                scope,
508                resultCollector,
509                null);
510        // Class declaration
511        pattern = new TypeDeclarationPattern(
512                null,
513                null,
514                null,
515                IIndexConstants.CLASS_SUFFIX,
516                SearchPattern.R_PATTERN_MATCH
517        );
518        new SearchEngine(new IJavaScriptUnit[] {workingCopies[0]}).search(
519                pattern,
520                new SearchParticipant[] {SearchEngine.getDefaultSearchParticipant()},
521                scope,
522                resultCollector,
523                null);
524        assertSearchResults(
525                "src/b73696/I.java b73696.I [I] EXACT_MATCH\n" + 
526                "src/b73696/C.java b73696.C [C] EXACT_MATCH"
527        );

587/**

591private void setUpBug77093() throws CoreException {
592        workingCopies = new IJavaScriptUnit[1];
593        workingCopies[0] = getWorkingCopy("/JavaSearchBugs/src/b77093/X.js",
594                "package b77093;\n" + 
595                "public class X {\n" + 
596                "        class Z {\n" + 
597                "        }\n" + 
598                "        Z[][] z_arrays;\n" + 
599                "        X() {\n" + 
600                "                this(new Z[10][]);\n" + 
601                "        }\n" + 
602                "        X(Z[][] arrays) {\n" + 
603                "                z_arrays = arrays;\n" + 
604                "        }\n" + 
605                "        private void foo(Z[] args) {\n" + 
606                "        }\n" + 
607                "        void bar() {\n" + 
608                "                for (int i=0; i<z_arrays.length; i++)\n" + 
609                "                        foo(z_arrays[i]);\n" + 
610                "        }\n" + 
611                "}"
612        );
613}
614public void testBug77093constructor() throws CoreException {
615        setUpBug77093();
616        IType type = workingCopies[0].getType("X");
617        IFunction method = type.getFunction("X", new String[] {"[[QZ;"});
618        // Search for constructor declarations and references
619        search(method, ALL_OCCURRENCES);
620        assertSearchResults(
621                "src/b77093/X.java b77093.X() [this(new Z[10][]);] EXACT_MATCH\n"+
622                "src/b77093/X.java b77093.X(Z[][]) [X] EXACT_MATCH"
623        );
624}
625public void testBug77093field() throws CoreException {

629        // Search for field declarations and references
630        search(field, ALL_OCCURRENCES);

1279/**
1280 * Bug 80890: [search] Strange search engine behaviour
1281 * @see "https://bugs.eclipse.org/bugs/show_bug.cgi?id=80890"
1282 */
1283public void testBug80890() throws CoreException, JavaScriptModelException {
1284        workingCopies = new IJavaScriptUnit[1];
1285        workingCopies[0] = getWorkingCopy("/JavaSearchBugs/src/b80890/A.js",
1286                "package b80890;\n" + 
1287                "public class A {\n" + 
1288                "        protected void foo(Exception e) {}\n" + 
1289                "        protected void foo(String s) {}\n" + 
1290                "}\n" + 
1291                "class B1 extends A {\n" + 
1292                "        public void bar1() {\n" + 
1293                "                foo(null);\n" + 
1294                "        }\n" + 
1295                "}\n" + 
1296                "class B2 extends A {\n" + 
1297                "        public void bar2() {\n" + 
1298                "                foo(null);\n" + 
1299                "        }\n" + 
1300                "}\n"
1301                );
1302        // search for first and second method should both return 2 inaccurate matches
1303        IType type = workingCopies[0].getType("A");
1304        IFunction method = type.getFunctions()[0];
1305        search(method, REFERENCES);
1306        method = type.getFunctions()[1];
1307        search(method, REFERENCES);
1308        assertSearchResults(
1309                "src/b80890/A.java void b80890.B1.bar1() [foo(null)] POTENTIAL_MATCH\n" + 
1310                "src/b80890/A.java void b80890.B2.bar2() [foo(null)] POTENTIAL_MATCH\n" + 
1311                "src/b80890/A.java void b80890.B1.bar1() [foo(null)] POTENTIAL_MATCH\n" + 
1312                "src/b80890/A.java void b80890.B2.bar2() [foo(null)] POTENTIAL_MATCH"
1313        );
1314}

1329/**

1331 * @see "https://bugs.eclipse.org/bugs/show_bug.cgi?id=81084"
1332 */
1333public void testBug81084a() throws CoreException, JavaScriptModelException {
1334        workingCopies = new IJavaScriptUnit[1];
1335        workingCopies[0] = getWorkingCopy("/JavaSearchBugs/src/b81084a/Test.js",
1336                "package b81084a;\n" + 
1337                "class List<E> {}\n" +

1339                "        class Element{}\n" + 
1340                "        static class Inner {\n" + 
1341                "                private final List<Element> fList1;\n" + 
1342                "                private final List<Test.Element> fList2;\n" + 
1343                "                public Inner(List<Element> list) {\n" + 
1344                "                        fList1 = list;\n" + 
1345                "                        fList2 = list;\n" + 
1346                "                }\n" + 
1347                "        }\n" + 
1348                "}\n"
1349        );

1357                "src/b81084a/Test.java b81084a.Test$Inner(List<Element>) [fList2] EXACT_MATCH"
1358        );
1359}
1360public void testBug81084string() throws CoreException, JavaScriptModelException {
1361        workingCopies = new IJavaScriptUnit[1];
1362        workingCopies[0] = getWorkingCopy("/JavaSearchBugs/src/b81084a/Test.js",
1363                "package b81084a;\n" + 
1364                "class List<E> {}\n" + 
1365                "public class Test {\n" + 
1366                "        class Element{}\n" + 
1367                "        static class Inner {\n" + 
1368                "                private final List<Element> fList1;\n" + 
1369                "                private final List<Test.Element> fList2;\n" + 
1370                "                public Inner(List<Element> list) {\n" + 
1371                "                        fList1 = list;\n" + 
1372                "                        fList2 = list;\n" + 
1373                "                }\n" + 
1374                "        }\n" + 
1375                "}\n"
1376        );

3129/**
3130 * Bug 93392: [1.5][search][annot] search for annotation elements does not seem to be implemented yet
3131 * @see "https://bugs.eclipse.org/bugs/show_bug.cgi?id=93392"
3132 * 
3133 * Note that this test valid also:
3134 * Bug 94062: [1.5][search][annot] search for annotation elements incorrect match range
3135 * @see "https://bugs.eclipse.org/bugs/show_bug.cgi?id=94062"
3136 */
3137public void testBug93392() throws CoreException {
3138        TestCollector collector = new TestCollector();
3139        collector.showAccuracy = true;
3140        workingCopies = new IJavaScriptUnit[1];
3141        workingCopies[0] = getWorkingCopy("/JavaSearchBugs/src/b93392/Test.js",
3142                "package b93392;\n" + 
3143                "@interface Annot {\n" + 
3144                "        int value();\n" +
3145                "}\n" +
3146                "@Annot(41)\n" + 
3147                "public class Test {\n" + 
3148                "        @Annot(21)\n" + 
3149                "        int bar;\n" + 
3150                "        @Annot(10)\n" + 
3151                "        public void foo() {}\n" + 
3152                "}\n"
3153        );
3154        IType type = selectType(workingCopies[0], "Annot");
3155        IFunction method = type.getFunction("value", new String[0]);
3156        search(method, REFERENCES, getJavaSearchScopeBugs(), collector);
3157        assertSearchResults(
3158                "src/b93392/Test.java b93392.Test [41] EXACT_MATCH\n" + 
3159                "src/b93392/Test.java b93392.Test.bar [21] EXACT_MATCH\n" + 
3160                "src/b93392/Test.java void b93392.Test.foo() [10] EXACT_MATCH",
3161                collector
3162        );
3163        // Verify matches positions
3164        String source = workingCopies[0].getSource();
3165        String str = "@Annot(";
3166        // First match
3167        assertEquals("Invalid number of matches", 3, collector.matches.size());
3168        int index= source.indexOf(str)+str.length();
3169        assertEquals("Invalid offset for first match", index, ((SearchMatch)collector.matches.get(0)).getOffset());
3170        assertEquals("Invalid length for first match", 2, ((SearchMatch)collector.matches.get(0)).getLength());
3171        // Second match
3172        index= source.indexOf(str, index)+str.length();
3173        assertEquals("Invalid offset for second match", index, ((SearchMatch)collector.matches.get(1)).getOffset());
3174        assertEquals("Invalid length for second match", 2, ((SearchMatch)collector.matches.get(1)).getLength());
3175        // Last match
3176        index= source.indexOf(str, index)+str.length();
3177        assertEquals("Invalid offset for last match", index, ((SearchMatch)collector.matches.get(2)).getOffset());
3178        assertEquals("Invalid length for last match", 2, ((SearchMatch)collector.matches.get(2)).getLength());
3179}

3229

3233

3241                        "src/b94389/Test.java void b94389.Test.foo() [foo]",
3242                        collector
3243                );
3244        
3245                // Verify that all matches have correct occurence count
3246                int size = collector.matches.size();
3247                for (int i=0; i<size; i++) {
3248                        assertEquals("Invalid foo method occurence count (m="+(m+1)+")", i+1, ((SourceMethod) methods[i]).occurrenceCount);
3249                }
3250        }

4167                "}\n" + 
4168                "class Sub extends Test<String> {\n" + 
4169                "    public void foo(String str) {}\n" +

4172        );

4659/**
4660 * Bug 108088: [search] Inaccurate search match for method invocations with literal arguments
4661 * @see "https://bugs.eclipse.org/bugs/show_bug.cgi?id=108088"
4662 */
4663public void testBug108088() throws CoreException {
4664        IJavaScriptUnit unit = getCompilationUnit("JavaSearchBugs", "src", "b108088", "Test108088.js");
4665        IType type = unit.getType("A108088");
4666        IFunction method = type.getFunction("subroutine", new String[] { "F" });
4667        SearchPattern pattern = SearchPattern.createPattern(method, REFERENCES, EXACT_RULE);
4668        assertNotNull("Pattern should not be null", pattern);
4669        search(pattern, getJavaSearchScopeBugs(), resultCollector);
4670        assertSearchResults(
4671                "src/b108088/B108088.java void b108088.B108088.doit(A108088, String) [subroutine(1.2f)] EXACT_MATCH"
4672        );
4673}

5144                "public class AA {\n" +
5145                "        AA() {}\n" +
5146                "}\n"
5147        );
5148        workingCopies[1] = getWorkingCopy("/JavaSearchBugs/src/b110060/AAxx.js",
5149                "package b110060;\n" + 
5150                "public class AAxx {\n" +
5151                "        AAxx() {}\n" +
5152                "}\n"
5153        );
5154        workingCopies[2] = getWorkingCopy("/JavaSearchBugs/src/b110060/AxxAyy.js",
5155                "package b110060;\n" + 
5156                "public class AxxAyy {\n" +
5157                "        AxxAyy() {}\n" +
5158                "}\n"
5159        );
5160        workingCopies[3] = getWorkingCopy("/JavaSearchBugs/src/b110060/AxA.js",
5161                "package b110060;\n" + 
5162                "public class AxA {\n" +
5163                "        AxA() {}\n" +
5164                "}\n"
5165        );
5166        workingCopies[4] = getWorkingCopy("/JavaSearchBugs/src/b110060/Test.js",
5167                "package b110060;\n" + 
5168                "public class Test {\n" +
5169                "        AA aa = new AA();\n" + 
5170                "        AAxx aaxx = new AAxx();\n" + 
5171                "        AxA axa = new AxA();\n" + 
5172                "        AxxAyy axxayy = new AxxAyy();\n" +

5174        );

5176public void testBug110060_ConstructorPattern01() throws CoreException {
5177        setUpBug110060_ConstructorPattern();
5178        search("AA", CONSTRUCTOR, REFERENCES, SearchPattern.R_CAMELCASE_MATCH);
5179        assertSearchResults(

5447/**
5448 * @test Bug 110336: [plan][search] Should optionaly return the local variable for type reference
5449 * @see "https://bugs.eclipse.org/bugs/show_bug.cgi?id=110336"
5450 */
5451public void testBug110336a() throws CoreException {
5452        workingCopies = new IJavaScriptUnit[1];
5453        workingCopies[0] = getWorkingCopy("/JavaSearchBugs/src/b110336/Test.js",
5454                "package b110336;\n" + 
5455                "public class Test {\n" + 
5456                "        <TP extends Test> void method(Class<Test> clazz) {\n" + 
5457                "                Test localVar1 = new Test();\n" + 
5458                "                Class<Test> localVar2 = new Class<Test>();\n" + 
5459                "                localVar1.method(localVar2);\n" + 
5460                "        }\n" + 
5461                "}\n"
5462        );
5463        IType type = this.workingCopies[0].getType("Test");
5464        TypeReferencesCollector collector = new TypeReferencesCollector();
5465        search(type, REFERENCES, EXACT_RULE, getJavaSearchScopeBugs(), collector);
5466        assertSearchResults(
5467                "src/b110336/Test.java void b110336.Test.method(Class<Test>).TP [Test]\n" + 
5468                "src/b110336/Test.java void b110336.Test.method(Class<Test>).clazz [Test]\n" + 
5469                "src/b110336/Test.java void b110336.Test.method(Class<Test>).localVar1 [Test]\n" + 
5470                "src/b110336/Test.java void b110336.Test.method(Class<Test>).localVar1 [Test]\n" + 
5471                "src/b110336/Test.java void b110336.Test.method(Class<Test>).localVar2 [Test]\n" +

6260 */
6261public void testBug125178() throws CoreException {

6264        workingCopies = new IJavaScriptUnit[1];

6268                "public class X {\n" + 
6269                "        public static void main(String[] args) {\n" +

6271                "        }\n" +

6274                problemRequestor
6275        );
6276        assertEquals("CU Should not have any problem!",
6277                "----------\n" +
6278                "----------\n",
6279                problemRequestor.problems.toString()
6280        );
6281        
6282        // Get anonymous from
6283        IPackageFragment jar = getPackageFragment("JavaSearchBugs", "lib/b125178.jar", "pack.age");

6285        assertNotNull("We should have children for in default package of lib/b125178.jar", children);
6286        for (int i=0,l=children.length; i<l; i++) {
6287                assertTrue("Jar should only have class files!", children[i] instanceof ClassFile);
6288                IType type = ((ClassFile)children[i]).getType();
6289                if (type.isAnonymous()) {
6290                        search(type, REFERENCES);
6291                }
6292        }
6293        assertSearchResults(
6294                "" // no result expected
6295        );
6296}

6318                                char[] typeName = 
6319                                        CharOperation.concat(
6320                                                CharOperation.concatWith(enclosingTypeNames, '$'), 
6321                                                simpleTypeName,
6322                                                '$');
6323                                results.addElement(new String(CharOperation.concat(packageName, typeName, '.')));
6324                        }
6325                }
6326        }

6328        new SearchEngine().searchAllTypeNames(
6329                null,
6330                SearchPattern.R_EXACT_MATCH,
6331                null,
6332                SearchPattern.R_PATTERN_MATCH, // case insensitive
6333                TYPE,
6334                getJavaSearchScopeBugs(),
6335                requestor,
6336                IJavaScriptSearchConstants.WAIT_UNTIL_READY_TO_SEARCH,
6337                null
6338        );
6339        assertSearchResults(

6341                "b127628.Test127628",
6342                requestor);

6462/**
6463 * To get these tests search matches in a workspace, do NOT forget to modify files
6464 * to set them as working copies.
6465 *
6466 * @test Bug 137087: Open Type - missing matches when using mixed case pattern
6467 * @see "https://bugs.eclipse.org/bugs/show_bug.cgi?id=137087"
6468 */
6469public void testBug137087() throws CoreException {
6470        // Search CamelCase
6471        int matchRule = SearchPattern.R_CAMELCASE_MATCH;
6472        String pattern = "runtimeEx";
6473        search(pattern, TYPE, DECLARATIONS, matchRule);
6474        assertSearchResults(
6475                ""+ getExternalJCLPathString("1.5") + " java.lang.RuntimeException EXACT_MATCH"
6476        );
6477        // Search like UI does (ie. replace it with prefix if it's not a valid CamelCase)
6478        int validatedRule = SearchPattern.validateMatchRule(pattern, matchRule);
6479        if (validatedRule != matchRule) {
6480                matchRule = SearchPattern.R_PREFIX_MATCH;
6481        }
6482        search(pattern, TYPE, DECLARATIONS, matchRule);
6483        assertSearchResults(
6484                ""+ getExternalJCLPathString("1.5") + " java.lang.RuntimeException EXACT_MATCH\n" +
6485                ""+ getExternalJCLPathString("1.5") + " java.lang.RuntimeException EXACT_MATCH"
6486        );
6487}

6577                "" // expected no result as uppercase characters in pattern do not match any camelcase ones in existing types
6578        );

7331                "                        foo(); // valid match as A is abstract => does not override Abstract.foo()\n" + 
7332                "                }\n" + 
7333                "        }\n" + 
7334                "        class B extends A {\n" + 
7335                "                public void foo() {}\n" + 
7336                "                void b() {\n" + 
7337                "                        foo(); // valid match as B.foo() is the first override in sub-class\n" + 
7338                "                }\n" + 
7339                "        }\n" + 
7340                "        class C extends B {\n" + 
7341                "                public void foo() {}\n" + 
7342                "                void c() {\n" + 
7343                "                        foo(); // invalid match as C.foo() overrides Abstract.foo() \n" + 
7344                "                }\n" + 
7345                "        }\n" + 
7346                "}"
7347        );
7348        IFunction method = workingCopies[0].getType("Test").getType("Abstract").getFunction("foo", new String[0]);
7349        search(method, REFERENCES);
7350        assertSearchResults(
7351                "src/Test.java void Test$A.a() [foo()] EXACT_MATCH\n" + 
7352                "src/Test.java void Test$B.b() [foo()] EXACT_MATCH"
7353        );
7354}
7355public void testBug160301_Abstract3() throws CoreException {
7356        resultCollector.showRule = true;

7360                "        abstract class Abstract {\n" + 
7361                "                public abstract void foo();\n" + 
7362                "        }\n" + 
7363                "        class A extends Abstract {\n" +
